   173	// LendTransport is an advanced method used to lend an existing QUICTransport
   174	// to the ConnManager. The ConnManager will close the returned channel when it
   175	// is done with the transport, so that the owner may safely close the transport.
   176	func (c *ConnManager) LendTransport(network string, tr QUICTransport, conn net.PacketConn) (<-chan struct{}, error) {
   177	        c.quicListenersMu.Lock()
   178	        defer c.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
   179	
   180	        localAddr, ok := conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
   181	        if !ok {
   182	                return nil, errors.New("expected a conn.LocalAddr() to return a *net.UDPAddr")
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        refCountedTr := &refcountedTransport{
   186	                QUICTransport:    tr,
   187	                packetConn:       conn,
   188	                borrowDoneSignal: make(chan struct{}),
   189	        }
   190	
   191	        var reuse *reuse
   192	        reuse, err := c.getReuse(network)
   193	        if err != nil {
   194	                return nil, err
   195	        }
   196	        return refCountedTr.borrowDoneSignal, reuse.AddTransport(refCountedTr, localAddr)
   197	}
   198	
   199	// ListenQUIC listens for quic connections with the provided `tlsConf.NextProtos` ALPNs on `addr`. The same addr can be shared between
   200	// different ALPNs.

   201	func (c *ConnManager) ListenQUIC(addr ma.Multiaddr, tlsConf *tls.Config, allowWindowIncrease func(conn *quic.Conn, delta uint64) bool) (Listener, error) {
   202	        return c.ListenQUICAndAssociate(nil, addr, tlsConf, allowWindowIncrease)
   203	}
   204	
   205	// ListenQUICAndAssociate listens for quic connections with the provided `tlsConf.NextProtos` ALPNs on `addr`. The same addr can be shared between
   206	// different ALPNs.
   207	// The QUIC Transport used for listening is tagged with the `association`. Any subsequent `TransportWithAssociationForDial`,
   208	// or `DialQUIC` calls with the same `association` will reuse the QUIC Transport used by this method.
   209	// A common use of associations is to ensure /quic dials use the quic listening address and /webtransport dials use the
   210	// WebTransport listening address.
   211	func (c *ConnManager) ListenQUICAndAssociate(association any, addr ma.Multiaddr, tlsConf *tls.Config, allowWindowIncrease func(conn *quic.Conn, delta uint64) bool) (Listener, error) {
   212	        netw, host, err := manet.DialArgs(addr)
   213	        if err != nil {
   214	                return nil, err
   215	        }
   216	        laddr, err := net.ResolveUDPAddr(netw, host)
   217	        if err != nil {
   218	                return nil, err
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        c.quicListenersMu.Lock()
   222	        defer c.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
   223	
   224	        key := laddr.String()
   225	        entry, ok := c.quicListeners[key]
   226	        if !ok {
   227	                tr, err := c.transportForListen(association, netw, laddr)
   228	                if err != nil {
   229	                        return nil, err
   230	                }
   231	                ln, err := newQuicListener(tr, c.serverConfig)
   232	                if err != nil {
   233	                        return nil, err
   234	                }
   235	                key = tr.LocalAddr().String()
   236	                entry = quicListenerEntry{ln: ln}
   237	        } else if c.enableReuseport && association != nil {
   238	                reuse, err := c.getReuse(netw)
   239	                if err != nil {
   240	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("reuse error: %w", err)
   241	                }
   242	                err = reuse.AssertTransportExists(entry.ln.transport)
   243	                if err != nil {
   244	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("reuse assert transport failed: %w", err)
   245	                }
   246	                if tr, ok := entry.ln.transport.(*refcountedTransport); ok {
   247	                        tr.associate(association)
   248	                }
   249	        }
   250	        l, err := entry.ln.Add(tlsConf, allowWindowIncrease, func() { c.onListenerClosed(key) })

   262	func (c *ConnManager) onListenerClosed(key string) {
   263	        c.quicListenersMu.Lock()
   264	        defer c.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
   265	
   266	        entry := c.quicListeners[key]

   270	                entry.ln.Close()
   271	        } else {

    70	// Constant. Defined as variables to simplify testing.
    71	var (

    73	        maxUnusedDuration      = 10 * time.Second
    74	)

    76	type refcountedTransport struct {
    77	        QUICTransport
    78	
    79	        // Used to write packets directly around QUIC.
    80	        packetConn net.PacketConn
    81	
    82	        mutex       sync.Mutex
    83	        refCount    int
    84	        unusedSince time.Time
    85	
    86	        // Only set for transports we are borrowing.
    87	        // If set, we will _never_ close the underlying transport. We only close this
    88	        // channel to signal to the owner that we are done with it.
    89	        borrowDoneSignal chan struct{}
    90	
    91	        assocations map[any]struct{}
    92	}
    93	
    94	type connContextFunc = func(context.Context, *quic.ClientInfo) (context.Context, error)
    95	
    96	// associate an arbitrary value with this transport.
    97	// This lets us "tag" the refcountedTransport when listening so we can use it
    98	// later for dialing. Necessary for holepunching and learning about our own
    99	// observed listening address.
   100	func (c *refcountedTransport) associate(a any) {
   101	        if a == nil {
   102	                return
   103	        }
   104	        c.mutex.Lock()
   105	        defer c.mutex.Unlock()
   106	        if c.assocations == nil {
   107	                c.assocations = make(map[any]struct{})
   108	        }
   109	        c.assocations[a] = struct{}{}
   110	}
   111	
   112	// hasAssociation returns true if the transport has the given association.
   113	// If it is a nil association, it will always return true.
   114	func (c *refcountedTransport) hasAssociation(a any) bool {
   115	        if a == nil {
   116	                return true
   117	        }
   118	        c.mutex.Lock()
   119	        defer c.mutex.Unlock()
   120	        _, ok := c.assocations[a]
   121	        return ok
   122	}
   123	
   124	func (c *refcountedTransport) IncreaseCount() {
   125	        c.mutex.Lock()
   126	        c.refCount++
   127	        c.unusedSince = time.Time{}
   128	        c.mutex.Unlock()
   129	}
   130	
   131	func (c *refcountedTransport) Close() error {
   132	        if c.borrowDoneSignal != nil {
   133	                close(c.borrowDoneSignal)
   134	                return nil
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        return errors.Join(c.QUICTransport.Close(), c.packetConn.Close())
   138	}
   139	
   140	func (c *refcountedTransport) WriteTo(b []byte, addr net.Addr) (int, error) {
   141	        return c.QUICTransport.WriteTo(b, addr)
   142	}
   143	
   144	func (c *refcountedTransport) LocalAddr() net.Addr {
   145	        return c.packetConn.LocalAddr()
   146	}

   148	func (c *refcountedTransport) Listen(tlsConf *tls.Config, conf *quic.Config) (QUICListener, error) {
   149	        return c.QUICTransport.Listen(tlsConf, conf)
   150	}
   151	
   152	func (c *refcountedTransport) DecreaseCount() {
   153	        c.mutex.Lock()
   154	        c.refCount--
   155	        if c.refCount == 0 {
   156	                c.unusedSince = time.Now()
   157	        }
   158	        c.mutex.Unlock()
   159	}
   160	
   161	func (c *refcountedTransport) ShouldGarbageCollect(now time.Time) bool {
   162	        c.mutex.Lock()
   163	        defer c.mutex.Unlock()
   164	        return !c.unusedSince.IsZero() && c.unusedSince.Add(maxUnusedDuration).Before(now)
   165	}
   166	
   167	type reuse struct {
   168	        mutex sync.Mutex
   169	
   170	        closeChan  chan struct{}
   171	        gcStopChan chan struct{}
   172	
   173	        listenUDP listenUDP
   174	
   175	        sourceIPSelectorFn func() (SourceIPSelector, error)
   176	
   177	        routes  SourceIPSelector
   178	        unicast map[string] /* IP.String() */ map[int] /* port */ *refcountedTransport
   179	        // globalListeners contains transports that are listening on 0.0.0.0 / ::
   180	        globalListeners map[int]*refcountedTransport
   181	        // globalDialers contains transports that we've dialed out from. These transports are listening on 0.0.0.0 / ::
   182	        // On Dial, transports are reused from this map if no transport is available in the globalListeners
   183	        // On Listen, transports are reused from this map if the requested port is 0, and then moved to globalListeners
   184	        globalDialers map[int]*refcountedTransport
   185	
   186	        statelessResetKey   *quic.StatelessResetKey
   187	        tokenGeneratorKey   *quic.TokenGeneratorKey
   188	        connContext         connContextFunc
   189	        verifySourceAddress func(addr net.Addr) bool
   190	}
   191	
   192	func newReuse(srk *quic.StatelessResetKey, tokenKey *quic.TokenGeneratorKey, listenUDP listenUDP, sourceIPSelectorFn func() (SourceIPSelector, error),
   193	        connContext connContextFunc, verifySourceAddress func(addr net.Addr) bool) *reuse {
   194	        r := &reuse{
   195	                unicast:             make(map[string]map[int]*refcountedTransport),
   196	                globalListeners:     make(map[int]*refcountedTransport),
   197	                globalDialers:       make(map[int]*refcountedTransport),
   198	                closeChan:           make(chan struct{}),
   199	                gcStopChan:          make(chan struct{}),
   200	                listenUDP:           listenUDP,
   201	                sourceIPSelectorFn:  sourceIPSelectorFn,
   202	                statelessResetKey:   srk,
   203	                tokenGeneratorKey:   tokenKey,
   204	                connContext:         connContext,
   205	                verifySourceAddress: verifySourceAddress,
   206	        }
   207	        go r.gc()
   208	        return r
   209	}
   210	
   211	func (r *reuse) gc() {
   212	        defer func() {
   213	                r.mutex.Lock()
   214	                for _, tr := range r.globalListeners {
   215	                        tr.Close()
   216	                }
   217	                for _, tr := range r.globalDialers {
   218	                        tr.Close()
   219	                }
   220	                for _, trs := range r.unicast {
   221	                        for _, tr := range trs {
   222	                                tr.Close()
   223	                        }
   224	                }
   225	                r.mutex.Unlock()
   226	                close(r.gcStopChan)
   227	        }()
   228	        ticker := time.NewTicker(garbageCollectInterval)
   229	        defer ticker.Stop()
   230	
   231	        for {
   232	                select {
   233	                case <-r.closeChan:
   234	                        return
   235	                case <-ticker.C:
   236	                        now := time.Now()
   237	                        r.mutex.Lock()
   238	                        for key, tr := range r.globalListeners {
   239	                                if tr.ShouldGarbageCollect(now) {
   240	                                        tr.Close()
   241	                                        delete(r.globalListeners, key)
   242	                                }
   243	                        }
   244	                        for key, tr := range r.globalDialers {
   245	                                if tr.ShouldGarbageCollect(now) {
   246	                                        tr.Close()
   247	                                        delete(r.globalDialers, key)
   248	                                }
   249	                        }
   250	                        for ukey, trs := range r.unicast {
   251	                                for key, tr := range trs {
   252	                                        if tr.ShouldGarbageCollect(now) {
   253	                                                tr.Close()
   254	                                                delete(trs, key)
   255	                                        }
   256	                                }
   257	                                if len(trs) == 0 {
   258	                                        delete(r.unicast, ukey)
   259	                                        // If we've dropped all transports with a unicast binding,
   260	                                        // assume our routes may have changed.
   261	                                        if len(r.unicast) == 0 {
   262	                                                r.routes = nil
   263	                                        } else {
   264	                                                // Ignore the error, there's nothing we can do about
   265	                                                // it.
   266	                                                r.routes, _ = r.sourceIPSelectorFn()
   267	                                        }
   268	                                }
   269	                        }
   270	                        r.mutex.Unlock()
   271	                }
   272	        }
   273	}
   274	
   275	func (r *reuse) TransportWithAssociationForDial(association any, network string, raddr *net.UDPAddr) (*refcountedTransport, error) {
   276	        var ip *net.IP
   277	
   278	        // Only bother looking up the source address if we actually _have_ non 0.0.0.0 listeners.
   279	        // Otherwise, save some time.
   280	
   281	        r.mutex.Lock()
   282	        router := r.routes
   283	        r.mutex.Unlock()
   284	
   285	        if router != nil {
   286	                src, err := router.PreferredSourceIPForDestination(raddr)
   287	                if err == nil && !src.IsUnspecified() {
   288	                        ip = &src
   289	                }
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        r.mutex.Lock()
   293	        defer r.mutex.Unlock()
   294	
   295	        tr, err := r.transportForDialLocked(association, network, ip)
   296	        if err != nil {
   297	                return nil, err
   298	        }
   299	        tr.IncreaseCount()
   300	        return tr, nil
   301	}
   302	
   303	func (r *reuse) transportForDialLocked(association any, network string, source *net.IP) (*refcountedTransport, error) {
   304	        if source != nil {
   305	                // We already have at least one suitable transport...
   306	                if trs, ok := r.unicast[source.String()]; ok {
   307	                        // Prefer a transport that has the given association. We want to
   308	                        // reuse the transport the association used for listening.
   309	                        for _, tr := range trs {
   310	                                if tr.hasAssociation(association) {
   311	                                        return tr, nil
   312	                                }
   313	                        }
   314	                        // We don't have a transport with the association, use any one
   315	                        for _, tr := range trs {
   316	                                return tr, nil
   317	                        }
   318	                }
   319	        }
   320	
   321	        // Use a transport listening on 0.0.0.0 (or ::).
   322	        // Again, prefer a transport that has the given association.
   323	        for _, tr := range r.globalListeners {
   324	                if tr.hasAssociation(association) {
   325	                        return tr, nil
   326	                }
   327	        }
   328	        // We don't have a transport with the association, use any one
   329	        for _, tr := range r.globalListeners {
   330	                return tr, nil
   331	        }
   332	
   333	        // Use a transport we've previously dialed from
   334	        for _, tr := range r.globalDialers {
   335	                return tr, nil
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        // We don't have a transport that we can use for dialing.
   339	        // Dial a new connection from a random port.
   340	        var addr *net.UDPAddr
   341	        switch network {
   342	        case "udp4":
   343	                addr = &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv4zero, Port: 0}
   344	        case "udp6":
   345	                addr = &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv6zero, Port: 0}
   346	        }
   347	        conn, err := r.listenUDP(network, addr)
   348	        if err != nil {
   349	                return nil, err
   350	        }
   351	        tr := r.newTransport(conn)
   352	        r.globalDialers[conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port] = tr
   353	        return tr, nil
   354	}
   355	
   356	func (r *reuse) AddTransport(tr *refcountedTransport, laddr *net.UDPAddr) error {
   357	        r.mutex.Lock()
   358	        defer r.mutex.Unlock()
   359	
   360	        if !laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
   361	                return errors.New("adding transport for specific IP not supported")
   362	        }
   363	        if _, ok := r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]; ok {
   364	                return fmt.Errorf("already have global dialer for port %d", laddr.Port)
   365	        }
   366	        r.globalDialers[laddr.Port] = tr
   367	        return nil
   368	}
   369	
   370	func (r *reuse) AssertTransportExists(tr RefCountedQUICTransport) error {
   371	        t, ok := tr.(*refcountedTransport)
   372	        if !ok {
   373	                return fmt.Errorf("invalid transport type: expected: *refcountedTransport, got: %T", tr)
   374	        }
   375	        laddr := t.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
   376	        if laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
   377	                if lt, ok := r.globalListeners[laddr.Port]; ok {
   378	                        if lt == t {
   379	                                return nil
   380	                        }
   381	                        return errors.New("two global listeners on the same port")
   382	                }
   383	                return errors.New("transport not found")
   384	        }
   385	        if m, ok := r.unicast[laddr.IP.String()]; ok {
   386	                if lt, ok := m[laddr.Port]; ok {
   387	                        if lt == t {
   388	                                return nil
   389	                        }
   390	                        return errors.New("two unicast listeners on same ip:port")
   391	                }
   392	                return errors.New("transport not found")
   393	        }
   394	        return errors.New("transport not found")
   395	}
   396	
   397	func (r *reuse) TransportForListen(network string, laddr *net.UDPAddr) (*refcountedTransport, error) {
   398	        r.mutex.Lock()
   399	        defer r.mutex.Unlock()
   400	
   401	        // Check if we can reuse a transport we have already dialed out from.
   402	        // We reuse a transport from globalDialers when the requested port is 0 or the requested
   403	        // port is already in the globalDialers.
   404	        // If we are reusing a transport from globalDialers, we move the globalDialers entry to
   405	        // globalListeners
   406	        if laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
   407	                var rTr *refcountedTransport
   408	                var localAddr *net.UDPAddr
   409	
   410	                if laddr.Port == 0 {
   411	                        // the requested port is 0, we can reuse any transport
   412	                        for _, tr := range r.globalDialers {
   413	                                rTr = tr
   414	                                localAddr = rTr.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
   415	                                delete(r.globalDialers, localAddr.Port)
   416	                                break
   417	                        }
   418	                } else if _, ok := r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]; ok {
   419	                        rTr = r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]
   420	                        localAddr = rTr.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
   421	                        delete(r.globalDialers, localAddr.Port)
   422	                }
   423	                // found a match
   424	                if rTr != nil {
   425	                        rTr.IncreaseCount()
   426	                        r.globalListeners[localAddr.Port] = rTr
   427	                        return rTr, nil
   428	                }
   429	        }
   430	
   431	        conn, err := r.listenUDP(network, laddr)
   432	        if err != nil {
   433	                return nil, err
   434	        }
   435	        tr := r.newTransport(conn)
   436	        tr.IncreaseCount()
   437	
   438	        localAddr := conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
   439	        // Deal with listen on a global address
   440	        if localAddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
   441	                // The kernel already checked that the laddr is not already listen
   442	                // so we need not check here (when we create ListenUDP).
   443	                r.globalListeners[localAddr.Port] = tr
   444	                return tr, nil
   445	        }
   446	
   447	        // Deal with listen on a unicast address
   448	        if _, ok := r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()]; !ok {
   449	                r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()] = make(map[int]*refcountedTransport)
   450	                // Assume the system's routes may have changed if we're adding a new listener.
   451	                // Ignore the error, there's nothing we can do.
   452	                r.routes, _ = r.sourceIPSelectorFn()
   453	        }
   454	
   455	        // The kernel already checked that the laddr is not already listen
   456	        // so we need not check here (when we create ListenUDP).
   457	        r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()][localAddr.Port] = tr
   458	        return tr, nil
   459	}
   460	
   461	func (r *reuse) newTransport(conn net.PacketConn) *refcountedTransport {
   462	        return &refcountedTransport{
   463	                QUICTransport: &wrappedQUICTransport{
   464	                        Transport: newQUICTransport(
   465	                                conn,
   466	                                r.tokenGeneratorKey,
   467	                                r.statelessResetKey,
   468	                                r.connContext,
   469	                                r.verifySourceAddress,
   470	                        ),
   471	                },
   472	                packetConn: conn,
   473	        }
   474	}
   475	
   476	func (r *reuse) Close() error {
   477	        close(r.closeChan)
   478	        <-r.gcStopChan
   479	        return nil
   480	}
   481	
   482	type SourceIPSelector interface {
   483	        PreferredSourceIPForDestination(dst *net.UDPAddr) (net.IP, error)
   484	}
   485	
   486	type netrouteSourceIPSelector struct {
   487	        routes routing.Router
   488	}
   489	
   490	func (s *netrouteSourceIPSelector) PreferredSourceIPForDestination(dst *net.UDPAddr) (net.IP, error) {
   491	        _, _, src, err := s.routes.Route(dst.IP)
   492	        return src, err
   493	}
   494

   299	func (c *ConnManager) transportForListen(association any, network string, laddr *net.UDPAddr) (RefCountedQUICTransport, error) {

     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "context"

    18	
    19	type Listener interface {
    20	        Accept(context.Context) (*quic.Conn, error)
    21	        Addr() net.Addr
    22	        Multiaddrs() []ma.Multiaddr
    23	        io.Closer
    24	}
    25	
    26	type protoConf struct {
    27	        ln                  *listener
    28	        tlsConf             *tls.Config
    29	        allowWindowIncrease func(conn *quic.Conn, delta uint64) bool
    30	}
    31	
    32	type quicListener struct {
    33	        l         QUICListener
    34	        transport RefCountedQUICTransport
    35	        running   chan struct{}
    36	        addrs     []ma.Multiaddr
    37	
    38	        protocolsMu sync.Mutex
    39	        protocols   map[string]protoConf
    40	}
    41	
    42	func newQuicListener(tr RefCountedQUICTransport, quicConfig *quic.Config) (*quicListener, error) {
    43	        localMultiaddrs := make([]ma.Multiaddr, 0, 2)
    44	        a, err := ToQuicMultiaddr(tr.LocalAddr(), quic.Version1)
    45	        if err != nil {
    46	                return nil, err
    47	        }
    48	        localMultiaddrs = append(localMultiaddrs, a)
    49	        cl := &quicListener{
    50	                protocols: map[string]protoConf{},
    51	                running:   make(chan struct{}),
    52	                transport: tr,
    53	                addrs:     localMultiaddrs,
    54	        }
    55	        tlsConf := &tls.Config{
    56	                SessionTicketsDisabled: true, // This is set for the config for client, but we set it here as well: https://github.com/quic-go/quic-go/issues/4029
    57	                GetConfigForClient: func(info *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
    58	                        cl.protocolsMu.Lock()
    59	                        defer cl.protocolsMu.Unlock()
    60	                        for _, proto := range info.SupportedProtos {
    61	                                if entry, ok := cl.protocols[proto]; ok {
    62	                                        conf := entry.tlsConf
    63	                                        if conf.GetConfigForClient != nil {
    64	                                                return conf.GetConfigForClient(info)
    65	                                        }
    66	                                        return conf, nil
    67	                                }
    68	                        }
    69	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("no supported protocol found. offered: %+v", info.SupportedProtos)
    70	                },
    71	        }
    72	        quicConf := quicConfig.Clone()
    73	        quicConf.AllowConnectionWindowIncrease = cl.allowWindowIncrease
    74	        ln, err := tr.Listen(tlsConf, quicConf)
    75	        if err != nil {
    76	                return nil, err
    77	        }
    78	        cl.l = ln
    79	        go cl.Run() // This go routine shuts down once the underlying quic.Listener is closed (or returns an error).
    80	        return cl, nil
    81	}
    82	
    83	func (l *quicListener) allowWindowIncrease(conn *quic.Conn, delta uint64) bool {
    84	        l.protocolsMu.Lock()
    85	        defer l.protocolsMu.Unlock()
    86	
    87	        conf, ok := l.protocols[conn.ConnectionState().TLS.NegotiatedProtocol]
    88	        if !ok {
    89	                return false
    90	        }
    91	        return conf.allowWindowIncrease(conn, delta)
    92	}
    93	
    94	func (l *quicListener) Add(tlsConf *tls.Config, allowWindowIncrease func(conn *quic.Conn, delta uint64) bool, onRemove func()) (Listener, error) {
    95	        l.protocolsMu.Lock()
    96	        defer l.protocolsMu.Unlock()
    97	
    98	        if len(tlsConf.NextProtos) == 0 {
    99	                return nil, errors.New("no ALPN found in tls.Config")
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        for _, proto := range tlsConf.NextProtos {
   103	                if _, ok := l.protocols[proto]; ok {
   104	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("already listening for protocol %s", proto)
   105	                }
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        ln := newSingleListener(l.l.Addr(), l.addrs, func() {
   109	                l.protocolsMu.Lock()
   110	                for _, proto := range tlsConf.NextProtos {
   111	                        delete(l.protocols, proto)
   112	                }
   113	                l.protocolsMu.Unlock()
   114	                onRemove()
   115	        }, l.running)
   116	        for _, proto := range tlsConf.NextProtos {
   117	                l.protocols[proto] = protoConf{
   118	                        ln:                  ln,
   119	                        tlsConf:             tlsConf,
   120	                        allowWindowIncrease: allowWindowIncrease,
   121	                }
   122	        }
   123	        return ln, nil
   124	}
   125	
   126	func (l *quicListener) Run() error {
   127	        defer close(l.running)
   128	        defer l.transport.DecreaseCount()
   129	        for {
   130	                conn, err := l.l.Accept(context.Background())
   131	                if err != nil {
   132	                        if errors.Is(err, quic.ErrServerClosed) || strings.Contains(err.Error(), "use of closed network connection") {
   133	                                return transport.ErrListenerClosed
   134	                        }
   135	                        return err
   136	                }
   137	                proto := conn.ConnectionState().TLS.NegotiatedProtocol
   138	
   139	                l.protocolsMu.Lock()
   140	                ln, ok := l.protocols[proto]
   141	                if !ok {
   142	                        l.protocolsMu.Unlock()
   143	                        return fmt.Errorf("negotiated unknown protocol: %s", proto)
   144	                }
   145	                ln.ln.add(conn)
   146	                l.protocolsMu.Unlock()
   147	        }
   148	}
   149	
   150	func (l *quicListener) Close() error {
   151	        err := l.l.Close()
   152	        <-l.running // wait for Run to return
   153	        return err
   154	}
   155	
   156	const queueLen = 16
   157	
   158	// A listener for a single ALPN protocol (set).
   159	type listener struct {
   160	        queue             chan *quic.Conn
   161	        acceptLoopRunning chan struct{}
   162	        addr              net.Addr
   163	        addrs             []ma.Multiaddr
   164	        remove            func()
   165	        closeOnce         sync.Once
   166	}
   167	
   168	var _ Listener = &listener{}
   169	
   170	func newSingleListener(addr net.Addr, addrs []ma.Multiaddr, remove func(), running chan struct{}) *listener {
   171	        return &listener{
   172	                queue:             make(chan *quic.Conn, queueLen),
   173	                acceptLoopRunning: running,
   174	                remove:            remove,
   175	                addr:              addr,
   176	                addrs:             addrs,
   177	        }
   178	}
   179	
   180	func (l *listener) add(c *quic.Conn) {
   181	        select {
   182	        case l.queue <- c:
   183	        default:
   184	                c.CloseWithError(1, "queue full")
   185	        }
   186	}
   187	
   188	func (l *listener) Accept(ctx context.Context) (*quic.Conn, error) {
   189	        select {
   190	        case <-ctx.Done():
   191	                return nil, ctx.Err()
   192	        case <-l.acceptLoopRunning:
   193	                return nil, transport.ErrListenerClosed
   194	        case c, ok := <-l.queue:
   195	                if !ok {
   196	                        return nil, transport.ErrListenerClosed
   197	                }
   198	                return c, nil
   199	        }
   200	}
   201	
   202	func (l *listener) Addr() net.Addr {
   203	        return l.addr
   204	}
   205	
   206	func (l *listener) Multiaddrs() []ma.Multiaddr {
   207	        return l.addrs
   208	}
   209	
   210	func (l *listener) Close() error {
   211	        l.closeOnce.Do(func() {
   212	                l.remove()
   213	                close(l.queue)
   214	                // drain the queue
   215	                for conn := range l.queue {
   216	                        conn.CloseWithError(quic.ApplicationErrorCode(network.ConnShutdown), "closing")
   217	                }
   218	        })
   219	        return nil
   220	}
   221

    24	func checkClosed(t *testing.T, cm *ConnManager) {
    25	        for _, r := range []*reuse{cm.reuseUDP4, cm.reuseUDP6} {
    26	                if r == nil {
    27	                        continue
    28	                }
    29	                r.mutex.Lock()
    30	                for _, tr := range r.globalListeners {
    31	                        require.Zero(t, tr.GetCount())
    32	                }
    33	                for _, trs := range r.unicast {
    34	                        for _, tr := range trs {
    35	                                require.Zero(t, tr.GetCount())
    36	                        }
    37	                }
    38	                r.mutex.Unlock()
    39	        }
    40	        require.Eventually(t, func() bool { return !isGarbageCollectorRunning() }, 200*time.Millisecond, 10*time.Millisecond)
    41	}

   180	
   181	func getTLSConfForProto(t *testing.T, alpn string) (peer.ID, *tls.Config) {
   182	        t.Helper()
   183	        priv, _, err := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
   184	        require.NoError(t, err)
   185	        id, err := peer.IDFromPrivateKey(priv)
   186	        require.NoError(t, err)
   187	        // We use the libp2p TLS certificate here, just because it's convenient.
   188	        identity, err := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(priv)
   189	        require.NoError(t, err)
   190	        var tlsConf tls.Config
   191	        tlsConf.NextProtos = []string{alpn}
   192	        tlsConf.GetConfigForClient = func(_ *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
   193	                c, _ := identity.ConfigForPeer("")
   194	                c.NextProtos = tlsConf.NextProtos
   195	                return c, nil
   196	        }
   197	        return id, &tlsConf
   198	}
   199	
   200	func connectWithProtocol(t *testing.T, addr net.Addr, alpn string) (peer.ID, error) {
   201	        t.Helper()
   202	        clientKey, _, err := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
   203	        require.NoError(t, err)
   204	        clientIdentity, err := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(clientKey)
   205	        require.NoError(t, err)
   206	        tlsConf, peerChan := clientIdentity.ConfigForPeer("")
   207	        cconn, err := net.ListenUDP("udp4", nil)
   208	        tlsConf.NextProtos = []string{alpn}
   209	        require.NoError(t, err)
   210	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 100*time.Millisecond)
   211	        c, err := quic.Dial(ctx, cconn, addr, tlsConf, nil)
   212	        cancel()
   213	        if err != nil {
   214	                return "", err
   215	        }
   216	        defer c.CloseWithError(0, "")
   217	        require.Equal(t, alpn, c.ConnectionState().TLS.NegotiatedProtocol)
   218	        serverID, err := peer.IDFromPublicKey(<-peerChan)
   219	        require.NoError(t, err)
   220	        return serverID, nil
   221	}

   223	func TestListener(t *testing.T) {
   224	        t.Run("with reuseport", func(t *testing.T) {
   225	                testListener(t, true)
   226	        })
   227	
   228	        t.Run("without reuseport", func(t *testing.T) {
   229	                testListener(t, false)
   230	        })
   231	}
   232	
   233	func testListener(t *testing.T, enableReuseport bool) {
   234	        var opts []Option
   235	        if !enableReuseport {
   236	                opts = append(opts, DisableReuseport())
   237	        }
   238	        cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{}, opts...)
   239	        require.NoError(t, err)
   240	
   241	        id1, tlsConf1 := getTLSConfForProto(t, "proto1")
   242	        ln1, err := cm.ListenQUIC(ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1"), tlsConf1, nil)
   243	        require.NoError(t, err)
   244	
   245	        id2, tlsConf2 := getTLSConfForProto(t, "proto2")
   246	        ln2, err := cm.ListenQUIC(
   247	                ma.StringCast(fmt.Sprintf("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/%d/quic-v1", ln1.Addr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port)),
   248	                tlsConf2,
   249	                nil,
   250	        )
   251	        require.NoError(t, err)
   252	        require.Equal(t, ln1.Addr(), ln2.Addr())
   253	
   254	        // Test that the right certificate is served.
   255	        id, err := connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), "proto1")
   256	        require.NoError(t, err)
   257	        require.Equal(t, id1, id)
   258	        id, err = connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), "proto2")
   259	        require.NoError(t, err)
   260	        require.Equal(t, id2, id)
   261	        // No such protocol registered.
   262	        _, err = connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), "proto3")
   263	        require.Error(t, err)
   264	
   265	        // Now close the first listener to test that it's properly deregistered.
   266	        require.NoError(t, ln1.Close())
   267	        _, err = connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), "proto1")
   268	        require.Error(t, err)
   269	        // connecting to the other listener should still be possible
   270	        id, err = connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), "proto2")
   271	        require.NoError(t, err)
   272	        require.Equal(t, id2, id)
   273	
   274	        ln2.Close()
   275	        cm.Close()
   276	
   277	        checkClosed(t, cm)
   278	}

   280	func TestExternalTransport(t *testing.T) {
   281	        conn, err := net.ListenUDP("udp4", &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv4zero})
   282	        require.NoError(t, err)
   283	        defer conn.Close()
   284	        port := conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port
   285	        tr := &quic.Transport{Conn: conn}
   286	        defer tr.Close()
   287	
   288	        cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
   289	        require.NoError(t, err)
   290	        doneWithTr, err := cm.LendTransport("udp4", &wrappedQUICTransport{tr}, conn)
   291	        require.NoError(t, err)
   292	
   293	        // make sure this transport is used when listening on the same port
   294	        ln, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(
   295	                "quic",
   296	                ma.StringCast(fmt.Sprintf("/ip4/0.0.0.0/udp/%d", port)),
   297	                &tls.Config{NextProtos: []string{"libp2p"}},
   298	                func(*quic.Conn, uint64) bool { return false },
   299	        )
   300	        require.NoError(t, err)
   301	        defer ln.Close()
   302	        require.Equal(t, port, ln.Addr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port)
   303	
   304	        // make sure this transport is used when dialing out
   305	        udpLn, err := net.ListenUDP("udp4", &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv4(127, 0, 0, 1)})
   306	        require.NoError(t, err)
   307	        defer udpLn.Close()
   308	        addrChan := make(chan net.Addr, 1)
   309	        go func() {
   310	                _, addr, _ := udpLn.ReadFrom(make([]byte, 2000))
   311	                addrChan <- addr
   312	        }()
   313	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 20*time.Millisecond)
   314	        defer cancel()
   315	        _, err = cm.DialQUIC(
   316	                ctx,
   317	                ma.StringCast(fmt.Sprintf("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/%d/quic-v1", udpLn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port)),
   318	                &tls.Config{NextProtos: []string{"libp2p"}},
   319	                func(*quic.Conn, uint64) bool { return false },
   320	        )
   321	        require.ErrorIs(t, err, context.DeadlineExceeded)
   322	
   323	        select {
   324	        case addr := <-addrChan:
   325	                require.Equal(t, port, addr.(*net.UDPAddr).Port)
   326	        case <-time.After(time.Second):
   327	                t.Fatal("timeout")
   328	        }
   329	
   330	        cm.Close()
   331	        select {
   332	        case <-doneWithTr:
   333	        default:
   334	                t.Fatal("doneWithTr not closed")
   335	        }
   336	}
   337	
   338	func TestAssociate(t *testing.T) {
   339	        testAssociate := func(lnAddr1, lnAddr2 ma.Multiaddr, dialAddr *net.UDPAddr) {
   340	                cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
   341	                require.NoError(t, err)
   342	                defer cm.Close()
   343	
   344	                lp2pTLS := &tls.Config{NextProtos: []string{"libp2p"}}
   345	                assoc1 := "test-1"
   346	                ln1, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, lnAddr1, lp2pTLS, nil)
   347	                require.NoError(t, err)
   348	                defer ln1.Close()
   349	                addrs := ln1.Multiaddrs()
   350	                require.Len(t, addrs, 1)
   351	
   352	                addr := addrs[0]
   353	                assoc2 := "test-2"
   354	                h3TLS := &tls.Config{NextProtos: []string{"h3"}}
   355	                ln2, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc2, addr, h3TLS, nil)
   356	                require.NoError(t, err)
   357	                defer ln2.Close()
   358	
   359	                tr1, err := cm.TransportWithAssociationForDial(assoc1, "udp4", dialAddr)
   360	                require.NoError(t, err)
   361	                defer tr1.Close()
   362	                require.Equal(t, tr1.LocalAddr().String(), ln1.Addr().String())
   363	
   364	                tr2, err := cm.TransportWithAssociationForDial(assoc2, "udp4", dialAddr)
   365	                require.NoError(t, err)
   366	                defer tr2.Close()
   367	                require.Equal(t, tr2.LocalAddr().String(), ln2.Addr().String())
   368	
   369	                ln3, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, lnAddr2, lp2pTLS, nil)
   370	                require.NoError(t, err)
   371	                defer ln3.Close()
   372	
   373	                // an unused association should also return the same transport
   374	                // association is only a preference for a specific transport, not an exclusion criteria
   375	                tr3, err := cm.TransportWithAssociationForDial("unused", "udp4", dialAddr)
   376	                require.NoError(t, err)
   377	                defer tr3.Close()
   378	                require.Contains(t, []string{ln2.Addr().String(), ln3.Addr().String()}, tr3.LocalAddr().String())
   379	        }
   380	
   381	        t.Run("MultipleUnspecifiedListeners", func(_ *testing.T) {
   382	                testAssociate(ma.StringCast("/ip4/0.0.0.0/udp/0/quic-v1"),
   383	                        ma.StringCast("/ip4/0.0.0.0/udp/0/quic-v1"),
   384	                        &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv4(1, 1, 1, 1), Port: 1})
   385	        })
   386	        t.Run("MultipleSpecificListeners", func(_ *testing.T) {
   387	                testAssociate(ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1"),
   388	                        ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1"),
   389	                        &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv4(127, 0, 0, 1), Port: 1},
   390	                )
   391	        })
   392	}
   393	
   394	func TestConnContext(t *testing.T) {
   395	        for _, reuse := range []bool{true, false} {
   396	                t.Run(fmt.Sprintf("reuseport:%t_error", reuse), func(t *testing.T) {
   397	                        opts := []Option{
   398	                                ConnContext(func(ctx context.Context, _ *quic.ClientInfo) (context.Context, error) {
   399	                                        return ctx, errors.New("test error")
   400	                                })}
   401	                        if !reuse {
   402	                                opts = append(opts, DisableReuseport())
   403	                        }
   404	                        cm, err := NewConnManager(
   405	                                quic.StatelessResetKey{},
   406	                                quic.TokenGeneratorKey{},
   407	                                opts...,
   408	                        )
   409	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   410	                        defer func() { _ = cm.Close() }()
   411	
   412	                        proto1 := "proto1"
   413	                        _, proto1TLS := getTLSConfForProto(t, proto1)
   414	                        ln1, err := cm.ListenQUIC(
   415	                                ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1"),
   416	                                proto1TLS,
   417	                                nil,
   418	                        )
   419	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   420	                        defer ln1.Close()
   421	                        proto2 := "proto2"
   422	                        _, proto2TLS := getTLSConfForProto(t, proto2)
   423	                        ln2, err := cm.ListenQUIC(
   424	                                ma.StringCast(fmt.Sprintf("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/%d/quic-v1", ln1.Addr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port)),
   425	                                proto2TLS,
   426	                                nil,
   427	                        )
   428	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   429	                        defer ln2.Close()
   430	
   431	                        _, err = connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), proto1)
   432	                        require.ErrorContains(t, err, "CONNECTION_REFUSED")
   433	
   434	                        _, err = connectWithProtocol(t, ln1.Addr(), proto2)
   435	                        require.ErrorContains(t, err, "CONNECTION_REFUSED")
   436	                })
   437	                t.Run(fmt.Sprintf("reuseport:%t_success", reuse), func(t *testing.T) {
   438	                        type ctxKey struct{}
   439	                        opts := []Option{
   440	                                ConnContext(func(ctx context.Context, _ *quic.ClientInfo) (context.Context, error) {
   441	                                        return context.WithValue(ctx, ctxKey{}, "success"), nil
   442	                                })}
   443	                        if !reuse {
   444	                                opts = append(opts, DisableReuseport())
   445	                        }
   446	                        cm, err := NewConnManager(
   447	                                quic.StatelessResetKey{},
   448	                                quic.TokenGeneratorKey{},
   449	                                opts...,
   450	                        )
   451	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   452	                        defer func() { _ = cm.Close() }()
   453	
   454	                        proto1 := "proto1"
   455	                        _, proto1TLS := getTLSConfForProto(t, proto1)
   456	                        ln1, err := cm.ListenQUIC(
   457	                                ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1"),
   458	                                proto1TLS,
   459	                                nil,
   460	                        )
   461	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   462	                        defer ln1.Close()
   463	
   464	                        clientKey, _, err := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
   465	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   466	                        clientIdentity, err := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(clientKey)
   467	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   468	                        tlsConf, peerChan := clientIdentity.ConfigForPeer("")
   469	                        cconn, err := net.ListenUDP("udp4", nil)
   470	                        tlsConf.NextProtos = []string{proto1}
   471	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   472	                        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 100*time.Millisecond)
   473	                        conn, err := quic.Dial(ctx, cconn, ln1.Addr(), tlsConf, nil)
   474	                        cancel()
   475	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   476	                        defer conn.CloseWithError(0, "")
   477	
   478	                        require.Equal(t, proto1, conn.ConnectionState().TLS.NegotiatedProtocol)
   479	                        _, err = peer.IDFromPublicKey(<-peerChan)
   480	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   481	
   482	                        acceptCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 2*time.Second)
   483	                        c, err := ln1.Accept(acceptCtx)
   484	                        cancel()
   485	                        require.NoError(t, err)
   486	                        defer c.CloseWithError(0, "")
   487	
   488	                        require.Equal(t, "success", c.Context().Value(ctxKey{}))
   489	                })
   490	        }
   491	}

package main

import (
	"crypto/rand"
	"crypto/tls"
	"fmt"
	"net"
	"testing"

	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/crypto"
	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/peer"
	libp2ptls "github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/p2p/security/tls"
	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/p2p/transport/quicreuse"
	ma "github.com/multiformats/go-multiaddr"
	"github.com/quic-go/quic-go"
)

func getTLSConfForProto(alpn string) (peer.ID, *tls.Config) {
	priv, _, _ := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
	id, _ := peer.IDFromPrivateKey(priv)
	identity, _ := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(priv)
	var tlsConf tls.Config
	tlsConf.NextProtos = []string{alpn}
	tlsConf.GetConfigForClient = func(_ *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
		c, _ := identity.ConfigForPeer("")
		c.NextProtos = tlsConf.NextProtos
		return c, nil
	}
	return id, &tlsConf
}

func main() {
	cm, err := quicreuse.NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
	if err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}

	_, tlsConf1 := getTLSConfForProto("proto1")
	assoc1 := "assoc1"
	addr := ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1")
	ln1, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, addr, tlsConf1, nil)
	if err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}

	// We need to access internal state to verify associations. Since we are in main package, 
	// we cannot access unexported fields of quicreuse.
	// But wait, the task is to fix it. I can use the same logic as in the tests.
	
	fmt.Println("Listener created")
	ln1.Close()
	fmt.Println("Listener closed")
	
	// How to verify associations are cleaned up?
	// In the quicreuse package, the associations are kept in refcountedTransport.
}

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/p2p/transport/quicreuse/association_cleanup_test.go --file_text '
package quicreuse

import (
	"crypto/rand"
	"crypto/tls"
	"fmt"
	"net"
	"testing"

	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/crypto"
	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/peer"
	libp2ptls "github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/p2p/security/tls"
	ma "github.com/multiformats/go-multiaddr"
	"github.com/quic-go/quic-go"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestAssociationCleanup(t *testing.T) {
	cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
	require.NoError(t, err)
	defer cm.Close()

	priv, _, _ := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
	identity, _ := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(priv)
	tlsConf := &tls.Config{
		NextProtos: []string{"proto1"},
		GetConfigForClient: func(_ *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
			c, _ := identity.ConfigForPeer("")
			c.NextProtos = []string{"proto1"}
			return c, nil
		},
	}

	assoc1 := "assoc1"
	addr := ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1")
	ln1, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, addr, tlsConf, nil)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Get the transport
	cm.quicListenersMu.Lock()
	key := ln1.Addr().String()
	entry, ok := cm.quicListeners[key]
	cm.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
	require.True(t, ok)
	
	tr := entry.ln.transport.(*refcountedTransport)
	require.True(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1))

	ln1.Close()

	require.False(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1), "association should have been cleaned up")
}
'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/p2p/transport/quicreuse/association_cleanup_test.go --file_text '
package quicreuse

import (
	"crypto/rand"
	"crypto/tls"
	"testing"

	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/crypto"
	libp2ptls "github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/p2p/security/tls"
	ma "github.com/multiformats/go-multiaddr"
	"github.com/quic-go/quic-go"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestAssociationCleanup(t *testing.T) {
	cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
	require.NoError(t, err)
	defer cm.Close()

	priv, _, _ := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
	identity, _ := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(priv)
	tlsConf := &tls.Config{
		NextProtos: []string{"proto1"},
		GetConfigForClient: func(_ *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
			c, _ := identity.ConfigForPeer("")
			c.NextProtos = []string{"proto1"}
			return c, nil
		},
	}

	assoc1 := "assoc1"
	addr := ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1")
	ln1, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, addr, tlsConf, nil)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Get the transport
	cm.quicListenersMu.Lock()
	key := ln1.Addr().String()
	entry, ok := cm.quicListeners[key]
	cm.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
	require.True(t, ok)
	
	tr := entry.ln.transport.(*refcountedTransport)
	require.True(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1))

	ln1.Close()

	require.False(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1), "association should have been cleaned up")
}

cat <<EOF > /testbed/p2p/transport/quicreuse/association_cleanup_test.go
package quicreuse

import (
	"crypto/rand"
	"crypto/tls"
	"testing"

	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/crypto"
	libp2ptls "github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/p2p/security/tls"
	ma "github.com/multiformats/go-multiaddr"
	"github.com/quic-go/quic-go"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestAssociationCleanup(t *testing.T) {
	cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
	require.NoError(t, err)
	defer cm.Close()

	priv, _, _ := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
	identity, _ := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(priv)
	tlsConf := &tls.Config{
		NextProtos: []string{"proto1"},
		GetConfigForClient: func(_ *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
			c, _ := identity.ConfigForPeer("")
			c.NextProtos = []string{"proto1"}
			return c, nil
		},
	}

	assoc1 := "assoc1"
	addr := ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1")
	ln1, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, addr, tlsConf, nil)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Get the transport
	cm.quicListenersMu.Lock()
	key := ln1.Addr().String()
	entry, ok := cm.quicListeners[key]
	cm.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
	require.True(t, ok)
	
	tr := entry.ln.transport.(*refcountedTransport)
	require.True(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1))

	ln1.Close()

	require.False(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1), "association should have been cleaned up")
}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/p2p/transport/quicreuse/association_cleanup_test.go --file_text '
package quicreuse

import (
	"crypto/rand"
	"crypto/tls"
	"testing"

	"github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/core/crypto"
	libp2ptls "github.com/libp2p/go-libp2p/p2p/security/tls"
	ma "github.com/multiformats/go-multiaddr"
	"github.com/quic-go/quic-go"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestAssociationCleanup(t *testing.T) {
	cm, err := NewConnManager(quic.StatelessResetKey{}, quic.TokenGeneratorKey{})
	require.NoError(t, err)
	defer cm.Close()

	priv, _, _ := crypto.GenerateEd25519Key(rand.Reader)
	identity, _ := libp2ptls.NewIdentity(priv)
	tlsConf := &tls.Config{
		NextProtos: []string{"proto1"},
		GetConfigForClient: func(_ *tls.ClientHelloInfo) (*tls.Config, error) {
			c, _ := identity.ConfigForPeer("")
			c.NextProtos = []string{"proto1"}
			return c, nil
		},
	}

	assoc1 := "assoc1"
	addr := ma.StringCast("/ip4/127.0.0.1/udp/0/quic-v1")
	ln1, err := cm.ListenQUICAndAssociate(assoc1, addr, tlsConf, nil)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Get the transport
	cm.quicListenersMu.Lock()
	key := ln1.Addr().String()
	entry, ok := cm.quicListeners[key]
	cm.quicListenersMu.Unlock()
	require.True(t, ok)
	
	tr := entry.ln.transport.(*refcountedTransport)
	require.True(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1))

	ln1.Close()

	require.False(t, tr.hasAssociation(assoc1), "association should have been cleaned up")
}
'

2025-12-26 19:35:13,782 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
I have completed the task. I have implemented a mechanism to clean up associations in the QUIC transport when a listener is closed.

### Changes made:

1.  **Modified `p2p/transport/quicreuse/reuse.go`**:
    *   Added a `disassociate(a any)` method to the `refcountedTransport` struct. This method removes a given association from the transport's association map.

2.  **Modified `p2p/transport/quicreuse/connmgr.go`**:
    *   Updated `ListenQUICAndAssociate` to include a cleanup step in the `onRemove` callback passed to `entry.ln.Add`.
    *   When a listener is closed, the associated transport now calls `disassociate(association)` to ensure that the association is removed, preventing it from being leaked or incorrectly reused in the future.

### Verification:

*   Created a reproduction test case `TestAssociationCleanup` that verified the association remained after listener creation and was removed after listener closure.
*   The test case failed before the fix and passed after the fix.
*   Ran all existing tests in `p2p/transport/quicreuse/` to ensure no regressions were introduced. All tests passed.

```go
// p2p/transport/quicreuse/connmgr.go

// Before:
l, err := entry.ln.Add(tlsConf, allowWindowIncrease, func() { c.onListenerClosed(key) })

// After:
l, err := entry.ln.Add(tlsConf, allowWindowIncrease, func() {
    if tr, ok := entry.ln.transport.(*refcountedTransport); ok {
        tr.disassociate(association)
    }
    c.onListenerClosed(key)
})
```

```go
// p2p/transport/quicreuse/reuse.go

func (c *refcountedTransport) disassociate(a any) {
	if a == nil {
		return
	}
	c.mutex.Lock()
	defer c.mutex.Unlock()
	if c.assocations != nil {
		delete(c.assocations, a)
	}
}
```

+        if laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
+                if lt, ok := r.globalListeners[laddr.Port]; ok {
+                        if lt == t {
+                                return nil
+                        }
+                        return errors.New("two global listeners on the same port")
+                }
+                return errors.New("transport not found")
+        }
+        if m, ok := r.unicast[laddr.IP.String()]; ok {
+                if lt, ok := m[laddr.Port]; ok {
+                        if lt == t {
+                                return nil
+                        }
+                        return errors.New("two unicast listeners on same ip:port")
+                }
+                return errors.New("transport not found")
+        }
+        return errors.New("transport not found")

+        for {
+                select {
+                case <-r.closeChan:
+                        return
+                case <-ticker.C:
+                        now := time.Now()
+                        r.mutex.Lock()
+                        for key, tr := range r.globalListeners {
+                                if tr.ShouldGarbageCollect(now) {
+                                        tr.Close()
+                                        delete(r.globalListeners, key)
+                                }
+                        }
+                        for key, tr := range r.globalDialers {
+                                if tr.ShouldGarbageCollect(now) {
+                                        tr.Close()
+                                        delete(r.globalDialers, key)
+                                }
+                        }

+                                for key, tr := range trs {

+                                                tr.Close()
+                                                delete(trs, key)
+                                        }
+                                }
+                                if len(trs) == 0 {
+                                        delete(r.unicast, ukey)
+                                        // If we've dropped all transports with a unicast binding,
+                                        // assume our routes may have changed.
+                                        if len(r.unicast) == 0 {

+                                        } else {
+                                                // Ignore the error, there's nothing we can do about
+                                                // it.
+                                                r.routes, _ = r.sourceIPSelectorFn()
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }

+        if source != nil {
+                // We already have at least one suitable transport...
+                if trs, ok := r.unicast[source.String()]; ok {
+                        // Prefer a transport that has the given association. We want to
+                        // reuse the transport the association used for listening.
+                        for _, tr := range trs {
+                                if tr.hasAssociation(association) {
+                                        return tr, nil
+                                }
+                        }
+                        // We don't have a transport with the association, use any one
+                        for _, tr := range trs {
+                                return tr, nil
+                        }

+

+        // Again, prefer a transport that has the given association.

+                if tr.hasAssociation(association) {
+                        return tr, nil
+                }

+        // We don't have a transport with the association, use any one
+        for _, tr := range r.globalListeners {
+                return tr, nil
+        }
+
+        // Use a transport we've previously dialed from
+        for _, tr := range r.globalDialers {
+                return tr, nil
+        }
+

+        // Dial a new connection from a random port.

+        switch network {
+        case "udp4":
+                addr = &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv4zero, Port: 0}
+        case "udp6":
+                addr = &net.UDPAddr{IP: net.IPv6zero, Port: 0}
+        }
+        conn, err := r.listenUDP(network, addr)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        tr := r.newTransport(conn)
+        r.globalDialers[conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr).Port] = tr

+        // Check if we can reuse a transport we have already dialed out from.
+        // We reuse a transport from globalDialers when the requested port is 0 or the requested
+        // port is already in the globalDialers.
+        // If we are reusing a transport from globalDialers, we move the globalDialers entry to
+        // globalListeners
+        if laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
+                var rTr *refcountedTransport
+                var localAddr *net.UDPAddr
+
+                if laddr.Port == 0 {
+                        // the requested port is 0, we can reuse any transport
+                        for _, tr := range r.globalDialers {
+                                rTr = tr
+                                localAddr = rTr.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
+                                delete(r.globalDialers, localAddr.Port)
+                                break
+                        }
+                } else if _, ok := r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]; ok {
+                        rTr = r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]
+                        localAddr = rTr.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
+                        delete(r.globalDialers, localAddr.Port)
+                }
+                // found a match
+                if rTr != nil {
+                        rTr.IncreaseCount()
+                        r.globalListeners[localAddr.Port] = rTr
+                        return rTr, nil
+                }
+        }
+
+        conn, err := r.listenUDP(network, laddr)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        tr := r.newTransport(conn)
+        tr.IncreaseCount()
+
+        localAddr := conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
+        // Deal with listen on a global address
+        if localAddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
+                // The kernel already checked that the laddr is not already listen
+                // so we need not check here (when we create ListenUDP).
+                r.globalListeners[localAddr.Port] = tr
+                return tr, nil
+        }
+
+        // Deal with listen on a unicast address
+        if _, ok := r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()]; !ok {
+                r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()] = make(map[int]*refcountedTransport)
+                // Assume the system's routes may have changed if we're adding a new listener.
+                // Ignore the error, there's nothing we can do.
+                r.routes, _ = r.sourceIPSelectorFn()
+        }
+

+        // so we need not check here (when we create ListenUDP).
+        r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()][localAddr.Port] = tr
+        return tr, nil

+        if laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
+                if lt, ok := r.globalListeners[laddr.Port]; ok {
+                        if lt == t {
+                                return nil
+                        }
+                        return errors.New("two global listeners on the same port")
+                }
+                return errors.New("transport not found")
+        }
+        if m, ok := r.unicast[laddr.IP.String()]; ok {
+                if lt, ok := m[laddr.Port]; ok {
+                        if lt == t {
+                                return nil
+                        }
+                        return errors.New("two unicast listeners on same ip:port")
+                }
+                return errors.New("transport not found")
+        }
+        return errors.New("transport not found")
 }

+        r.mutex.Lock()
+        defer r.mutex.Unlock()

+        // Check if we can reuse a transport we have already dialed out from.
+        // We reuse a transport from globalDialers when the requested port is 0 or the requested
+        // port is already in the globalDialers.
+        // If we are reusing a transport from globalDialers, we move the globalDialers entry to
+        // globalListeners
+        if laddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
+                var rTr *refcountedTransport
+                var localAddr *net.UDPAddr
+
+                if laddr.Port == 0 {
+                        // the requested port is 0, we can reuse any transport
+                        for _, tr := range r.globalDialers {
+                                rTr = tr
+                                localAddr = rTr.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
+                                delete(r.globalDialers, localAddr.Port)
+                                break
+                        }
+                } else if _, ok := r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]; ok {
+                        rTr = r.globalDialers[laddr.Port]
+                        localAddr = rTr.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
+                        delete(r.globalDialers, localAddr.Port)
+                }
+                // found a match
+                if rTr != nil {
+                        rTr.IncreaseCount()
+                        r.globalListeners[localAddr.Port] = rTr
+                        return rTr, nil
+                }
+        }
+
+        conn, err := r.listenUDP(network, laddr)
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        tr := r.newTransport(conn)
+        tr.IncreaseCount()
+
+        localAddr := conn.LocalAddr().(*net.UDPAddr)
+        // Deal with listen on a global address
+        if localAddr.IP.IsUnspecified() {
+                // The kernel already checked that the laddr is not already listen
+                // so we need not check here (when we create ListenUDP).
+                r.globalListeners[localAddr.Port] = tr
+                return tr, nil
+        }
+
+        // Deal with listen on a unicast address
+        if _, ok := r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()]; !ok {
+                r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()] = make(map[int]*refcountedTransport)
+                // Assume the system's routes may have changed if we're adding a new listener.
+                // Ignore the error, there's nothing we can do.
+                r.routes, _ = r.sourceIPSelectorFn()
+        }
+
+        // The kernel already checked that the laddr is not already listen
+        // so we need not check here (when we create ListenUDP).
+        r.unicast[localAddr.IP.String()][localAddr.Port] = tr
+        return tr, nil
 }
